can be bought or unlocked my league friends unfortunately never got it i had to keep playing league with them they refused to give the game more than a few hours each crushed me still bitter about that to this day my love for dota turned into a total obsession i learned as much as i could and played whenever i had the time i was so inspired by fear and dendi stories in free to play i wanted to go the distance myself i saw dota as the one path for me to turn my boundless enthusiasm for strategy games into freedom from jobs i didn t love and a place i didn t want to live the one rope i could use to pull upward into the future i wanted for myself of course i decided to become a professional dota player this wasn t meant to be i was working as a busboy at the time and would work my shift and come home at night and play then work again without any significant breaks i would go hrs without sleep regularly to play as much dota as i could without missing any work went to lan and placed nd that was one of my favorite experiences in my life also met people from all over the world and learned words mostly curses heh from languages i would have otherwise never encountered got to practice my spanish a bit too i grew so much as a person from the interactions i had in dota it shaped me despite my extreme and overzealous and counterproductive in retrospect dedication i never got above k mmr what happened instead was that i ended up in the mental hospital from playing between and ranked matches a day and not sleeping on top of working my full time job bussing tables which i worked as hard as i could at as well when i got to the hospital i was lbs i am and hadn t eaten or slept for days and was in full blown manic psychosis maybe if i had been provided for and fully supported during this time and born without bipolar disorder by my parents i could have done it we ll never know but that what happened what i did was the epitome of the adage burning the candle from both ends i flew too close to the sun and crashed and burned in the flames of psychosis and malnutrition it been almost years since that episode of mania don t worry guys i m fine now i sleep and eat every single day and have never had a recurrence of mania i use medication to stabilize my mood whenever that pattern fails although i still enjoy the game a lot i really only play turbo on and off since that what i have time for gone are the dreams i know i spent a lot of time on this game and i will regret somewhat my failure to become pro for the rest of my life at one point it was everything to me i lived breathed and dreamed it that said i look back on all that time with nostalgia and fondness this is a game that will one way or another leave an impression on the rest of your life you will either give up at less than hours or you will never forget it how can i not recommend that it a masterpiece p s here my dotabuff if you want to see my schedule during that breaking point

if you re looking for a game review you ve come to the wrong place but if youre looking for a fantastic ravioli recipe you ve come to the right place ingredients to make the dough grams cups plain flour teaspoon salt eggs cup ml tablespoons olive oil cup ml tablespoons water extra flour for dusting to make cheese filling ounces grams container ricotta cheese ounces g about cup plus tablespoons cheese italian blend parmesan romano asiago note grate these cheeses yourself and create your own custom blend cup cheddar cheese eggs lightly beaten teaspoon salt teaspoon pepper extras your favorite sauce for the ravioli i e marinara marijuana parmesan cheese basil fried vegetables shrimp fish slices chicken pieces make the ravioli filling in a small mixing bowl add the ricotta and mash with a fork add in the cheese blend cheddar cheese eggs salt and pepper mix all ingredients thoroughly until you have a smooth paste like consistency cover the bowl with plastic wrap and place it in the refrigerator for about minutes make the ravioli dough crack eggs into a large mixing bowl and beat them with a fork add water oil and salt mix add cup flour to the bowl use a fork to mix the flour with the eggs water oil and salt repeat with the rest of the flour mix until a smooth dough is formed clear and clean off a large work surface and dust it with flour this is where you are going to roll out your dough take the dough out of the mixing bowl shape it into a ball and place it on your work surface knead for at least minutes or until it becomes elastic dust a rolling pin with flour to prevent the dough from sticking roll out the dough until it is about inch cm thick or about the thickness of stacked quarters with a cookie cutter or upside down water glass cut out circles in the dough will make about dough circles ball up the unused dough and either roll it out and make a couple more raviolis or wrap it and put in the freezer for another time dough can keep for weeks when frozen just make sure to wrap well so that it doesn t suffer from freezer burn or absorb freezer odor fill the ravioli shells take the ravioli filling out of the refrigerator and place a tablespoon of it in middle of a dough fill a small bowl with water dip your fingers in and moisten around the outer edge of the dough circle fold the dough in half over the filling making a half moon shape be sure all the filling stays inside pinch the edges together and then seal the edges of the ravioli with a fork make sure to press firmly and go all the way around this will add a homemade touch as well repeat this process for all your dough circles dust the finished ravioli with flour to keep them from sticking together form the shells and fill using a ravioli maker roll the dough into two sheets place one sheet on the ravioli maker and form the filling cups fill with the ravioli mixture lay the second sheet of dough on top and roll it out this will seal in the filling remove and separate the finished raviolis cook the ravioli fill a large pot with water and bring to a boil place the ravioli in boiling water for minutes or until they float you can also test for doneness by nibbling on the edges to test if you don t want to make all the ravioli at one time you can freeze the rest take ravioli out of boiling water with large slotted spoon and place on warmed plates serve it up top with your favorite sauce grate some fresh cheese over it and enjoy the formuoli

dota is hard but there a huge reward for those who commit on the surface the game is a like for like reproduction of the genre creating and still updated defense of the ancients modification for warcraft iii now transferred into valve source engine the game punishing design is sometimes enough to drive you up the wall but it worth sticking the hours in success in dota is about learning to effectively juggle both the broad strokes and finer details if you re not aware of the basics of the burgeoning moba genre two teams of five players spawn on corners of a map each team needs to work together with the goal of ultimately destroying a central structure in dota case the ancient in the opposing team base with most games lasting around the minute mark and occasionally edging past an hour watching the enemy fortress dramatically crumble and sink to the ground feels like an exhilarating payoff aiding these two teams named the radiant and the dire are waves of ai assistants called creeps batches of creeps spawn at second intervals and charge merrily up the map three pathways in the clumps of remaining land lies a jungle where numerous ai opponents spawn offering lucrative benefits to players who take them on successfully finally and in a bid to stop both teams from simply marching into one another base each team gets three powerful towers on each lane that easily shred through enemy players at the start of the game your individual ability to control and affect the rhythm of the game comes from how well you handle your hero you mostly control a single unit in dota though there are exceptions some heroes can summon controllable allies such as bears gargoyle babies or wolves one exceptionally versatile hero can split into three and one item lets you take control of certain creeps for each rule in dota impressive house of cards design there usually at least one character who completely ignores it or finds a way around it via one of odd items available from the in match shop for instance try negating magic attacks with the black king bar returning damage with the blade mail or pounding out two ultimate abilities in quick succession with a refresher orb the aim for most players is to accumulate as much gold and experience as possible with income being delivered mostly by scoring the killing blow on enemy creeps and players it almost always easier to gang up on stray enemies as a group which is why it rarely a good idea to run about on your own then it a case of splashing all your hard earned money on some ultra powerful items from the shop while levelling up your base stats and abilities and then clobbering the enemy team into submission via a few five versus five team fights rarely does it feel that simple however at the time of writing of the original dota heroes have made their way into the sequel each hero has a handful of unique abilities and generally works best in a specific role such as supporting other players as omniknight roaming around the map looking for opportunistic kills as spirit breaker or evolving throughout the course of the game into an all powerful vehicle of carnage and destruction as phantom assassin there only one map unlike in many other moba titles although valve has not ruled out the addition of more over time and has previously offered game changing modes with seasonal events at halloween and christmas but dota single sprawling map sets itself apart from the competition by being larger more intricate and packed with greater detail than the rest of the genre unlike in league of legends the jungle area is riddled with far more tangling pathways the lanes feature additional shops selling exclusive items and savvy players are given more opportunities to use the environment to hide flee and ambush their opponents often the game dizzying scale is seen as off putting or simply too complex but the truth of dota is that it can be entertaining as a new player to just sit down and let all those extraneous factors play out around you getting down to the brass tacks of the game with a group of like minded friends is a lot of fun start by buying your characters recommended items try your best not to get caught out of position and get into the habit of buying observer wards and watch out for riki as you d expect from valve this is a beautifully presented game with the half life and portal maker running victory laps around its competition in terms of ui voice acting and showing how to deftly add real personality to its characters only recently has the developer turned its attention to gently easing new players into the proceedings however and even now mastering the basics feels like learning to swim by jumping in at the deep end efforts are being made to remedy this though right now there are a couple of tutorial levels some well designed ai bots and a newbie playlist that restricts hero selection to just of the most frequently picked characters and with community created hero guides now built directly into the game itself dota is much easier to get started with than it has been in the past play a match every evening for a couple of weeks and you start to see how dota wealth of disparate systems and mechanics combine into their own harmony and you begin to understand how there are hundreds of elements that affect the game dota is a tense war of accumulation and attrition the biggest problem which is coincidentally where the real excitement of the game lies comes from struggling to process and interpret dozens upon dozens of mitigating circumstances while simultaneously trying to keep your cool it is a complicated and exhausting game and for the first few weeks it challenging just keeping up with the general rhythm of a match but invest enough time into dota and you develop an almost unconscious ability to keep up with the game performing actions such as sending the slightly fiddly in game courier over to the faraway secret shop to get some rare items for instance after a couple of hundred hours of dota what once felt like spinning plates just happens automatically while dota has transferred the core of the original dota into a cleaner modern engine the fact remains that losing is uniquely painful death in dota not only gives your opponent money but robs you of some of your own and leaves you waiting up to a minute to respawn by the time you ve trudged back across the game massive map or spent money on a teleportation scroll your opponent is now stronger and richer die two or three times in quick succession which is easily done and a match of dota becomes a painful experience where you spend the next half hour getting bullied by an increasingly superior enemy other games in the genre have tried to mitigate this punishment but dota positively revels in its complexities the rich just get richer the original dota was an unexpectedly powerful blend of clashing genres and disparate elements that ended up taking over the world and valve successor retains the original rules and characters while adding in a cheery free to play model and slick production values the experience of playing dota changes day by day some evenings will be exhilarating while others will kick your morale to the curb but there are few games as worthy of your time investment as this those who choose to commit to dota will find many happy hours within this immaculate update

an existential review of dota or hell is other teammates one does not simply play dota one is condemned to it this digital artifact presented as a free to play game is in truth a meticulously crafted simulation of the human condition in its most agonizing and absurd form it is a universe where freedom is absolute yet one s essence is perpetually defined and nullified by the relentless gaze of four allies and five enemies to log into steam and queue for a match is to willingly enter a state of profound existential commitment from which there is no early exit without moral and numeric penalty i the weight of choice and the abyss of picking the torment begins not in battle but in the draft the player is presented with over a hundred heroes each a distinct set of possibilities and limitations this is not freedom but the vertigo of choice to random a selection is an act of bad faith a fleeing from one s responsibility to define oneself within the team s composition rewarded with trivial consumables as a bribe for abdication in the ranked all pick mode this drama becomes a social performance one votes to banish a hero into the void of the ban list projecting one s anxieties onto the anonymous other the picks are hidden a tense theatre where choosing the same hero as another results in a shared negation a tiny absurd conflict of consciousnesses before the game even begins the game offers modes that promise relief from this burden but they are illusions in single draft one s agency is reduced to a choice between four predetermined ontological categories strength agility intelligence universal in all random one s being is assigned by a blind uncaring system these are not respites but stark revelations whether chosen or assigned one is thrown into a role for which one may be fundamentally unsuited the hero is not a vehicle for expression but a facticity one must embody often inauthentically ii being toward death of the ancient the match itself is a slow collective suicide pact the stated goal to destroy the opposing ancient is a meaningless telos a macguffin that legitimizes fifty minutes of mutually assured frustration the true project is the ceaseless struggle to define oneself through action while being fundamentally de trop for one s teammates consider the core mechanics which are designed to manufacture anguish the practice of denying killing one s own ai units to starve the opponent is a profound metaphor it is an act of negative creation a destruction of one s own resources to negate the other s gain it renders the laning phase a nihilistic economy where value is derived from absence furthermore upon death a hero not only ceases to be but is robbed a portion of its accumulated gold stripped away this is not a setback it is a phenomenological reduction one s projects to buy a pivotal item are actively dismantled by the other making death not a mere interruption but an ontological theft the community speaks of a steep learning curve this is a euphemism the newcomer is not learning they are drowning in a sea of pre constituted knowledge item builds hero counters secret pull timers never explained by the game itself this knowledge forms the they self of dota an anonymous oppressive body of tradition that the player must internalize to be seen as legitimate to be new is to be perpetually in the wrong one s very being a source of irritation for the others who have submitted to the rules iii the gaze of the other and the toxicity of us it is here we arrive at the central truth of dota perfectly encapsulating my famous phrase hell is other people the game s architecture is a machine for producing this hell four other consciousnesses are shackled to your fate their freedom a permanent threat to your own a teammate s poor decision a feed is not a mistake it is a violation of your shared project an imposition of their flawed freedom upon your own the chat wheel the pings the purchase of a sentinel ward these are not communications but instruments of mutual objectification you are for your teammate the idiot carry or the useless support you are frozen in their judgment valve playing the role of a indifferent demiurge attempts to manage this hell with behavioral systems and matchmaking but this only adds another layer of abstraction to the conflict the report function is not justice it is the bureaucraticization of resentment one s conduct score becomes a numerical representation of one s being for others a public quantification of your desirability as a co condemned soul and what of the promised escapes turbo mode with its accelerated gold and weakened towers is a capitalist parody of happiness all reward no stakes a hollow frenzy that only highlights the meaninglessness of the original struggle to play against bots is to engage in a sterile pantomime where the other s resistance is a predictable fiction offering no threat and therefore no authentic engagement iv conclusion the flicker of freedom in the trench yet in this very absurdity a terrible exhilarating freedom persists for all its oppressive structures dota offers a field of action that is relentlessly pure with all heroes free and no gameplay advantage for sale the playing field is existentially level victory and defeat are distilled to the actions taken within the match in a single perfect team fight a coordinated eruption of spells where five consciousnesses briefly align as one there is a transcendence it is a fleeting moment of being for itself in a team where individual projects are subsumed into a collective victorious project this moment is the bait in the trap it is the reason millions return daily to this ocean deep pool of rewarding nuance and strategy to this modern multiplayer masterpiece that is also a factory of misery dota does not offer fun it offers significance it makes every decision every last hit every death feel agonizingly weighty it forces you to exist conspicuously and consequentially in the eyes of others therefore i cannot recommend dota nor can i advise against it it simply is a brutal beautiful and utterly sincere monument to the conflict at the heart of existence to play it is to understand that in a universe devoid of inherent meaning we create our own meaning and often we do so by desperately trying to destroy the meaning making project of the strangers on the other side of the river you will lose gold you will lose time you may lose your equanimity but for those who persist you will in the process confront the stark thrilling burden of your own freedom now if you will excuse me my team needs a support

if you came here looking for a review you came to the wrong place if you came here looking for a delicous pie recipe you came to the right place apple pie pounds mixed apples such as granny smith gala and mcintosh cup granulated sugar tablespoons fresh lemon juice tablespoons unsalted butter tablespoon all purpose flour plus more for dusting teaspoon ground cinnamon teaspoon salt disks dough for basic crust large egg beaten coarse sugar for sprinkling peel and core the apples slice inch thick toss with the granulated sugar and lemon juice heat tablespoons butter in a large skillet over medium high heat add the apples and cook stirring until tender about minutes stir in the flour cinnamon and salt cook until thickened more minute let cool roll out disk of dough into a inch round on a floured surface ease into a inch pie plate add the apples mounding them slightly in the center and dot with the remaining tablespoons butter roll out the remaining dough into a inch round lay it over the filling press the edges of the crusts together then fold the overhang under itself and crimp to seal brush with the beaten egg and sprinkle with coarse sugar cut a few slits in the top crust chill hour place a baking sheet on the lowest oven rack and preheat to degrees f for minutes place the pie on the hot baking sheet lower the temperature to degrees f bake until golden hour to hour minutes cover the edges with foil if they brown too quickly cool on a rack

if you re looking for a game review you ve come to the wrong place but if youre looking for a fantastic ravioli recipe you ve come to the right place ingredients to make the dough grams cups plain flour teaspoon salt eggs cup ml tablespoons olive oil cup ml tablespoons water extra flour for dusting to make cheese filling ounces grams container ricotta cheese ounces g about cup plus tablespoons cheese italian blend parmesan romano asiago note grate these cheeses yourself and create your own custom blend cup cheddar cheese eggs lightly beaten teaspoon salt teaspoon pepper extras your favorite sauce for the ravioli i e marinara marijuana parmesan cheese basil fried vegetables shrimp fish slices chicken pieces make the ravioli filling in a small mixing bowl add the ricotta and mash with a fork add in the cheese blend cheddar cheese eggs salt and pepper mix all ingredients thoroughly until you have a smooth paste like consistency cover the bowl with plastic wrap and place it in the refrigerator for about minutes make the ravioli dough crack eggs into a large mixing bowl and beat them with a fork add water oil and salt mix add cup flour to the bowl use a fork to mix the flour with the eggs water oil and salt repeat with the rest of the flour mix until a smooth dough is formed clear and clean off a large work surface and dust it with flour this is where you are going to roll out your dough take the dough out of the mixing bowl shape it into a ball and place it on your work surface knead for at least minutes or until it becomes elastic dust a rolling pin with flour to prevent the dough from sticking roll out the dough until it is about inch cm thick or about the thickness of stacked quarters with a cookie cutter or upside down water glass cut out circles in the dough will make about dough circles ball up the unused dough and either roll it out and make a couple more raviolis or wrap it and put in the freezer for another time dough can keep for weeks when frozen just make sure to wrap well so that it doesn t suffer from freezer burn or absorb freezer odor fill the ravioli shells take the ravioli filling out of the refrigerator and place a tablespoon of it in middle of a dough fill a small bowl with water dip your fingers in and moisten around the outer edge of the dough circle fold the dough in half over the filling making a half moon shape be sure all the filling stays inside pinch the edges together and then seal the edges of the ravioli with a fork make sure to press firmly and go all the way around this will add a homemade touch as well repeat this process for all your dough circles dust the finished ravioli with flour to keep them from sticking together form the shells and fill using a ravioli maker roll the dough into two sheets place one sheet on the ravioli maker and form the filling cups fill with the ravioli mixture lay the second sheet of dough on top and roll it out this will seal in the filling remove and separate the finished raviolis cook the ravioli fill a large pot with water and bring to a boil place the ravioli in boiling water for minutes or until they float you can also test for doneness by nibbling on the edges to test if you don t want to make all the ravioli at one time you can freeze the rest take ravioli out of boiling water with large slotted spoon and place on warmed plates serve it up top with your favorite sauce grate some fresh cheese over it and enjoy

i ve spent years and almost hours playing warcraft iii dota as well as dota and loved playing it i ve met many interesting people fought epic battles snatched victory from the jaws of defeat through several herculean efforts endured many soul crushing defeats and even clashed with a handful of professional players the game has changed drastically over my many years of playing but as of about a year ago the game became too frustrating to continue and as i continue to watch i am saddened by what the game has become for years my friends and i have joked about the league ification of dota dota has always been the epitome of hyper competitive cooperative gameplay with a high emphasis on individual skill and decision making at all phases of the game especially in punishing poor decisions pushing a tower alone with nobody showing on the map get back or you re dead hard carry dies past minutes without buyback that a barracks down pick crappy laning heroes welcome to hell while the enemy team runs a trilane and pushes barracks at minutes our jokes slowly but surely became a reality teleport scrolls were reduced in cost meaning everybody rolled around with a handful because they weren t a financial burden ways to gain gold were increased so supports could afford to have a handful of items in the mid game the rubber band effect was introduced and pushing strategies were neutered you pick a lineup to take towers and take one unfavorable engagement and the game over whereas previously the greedier lineup would have to do more work than a single fight to overcome the gold advantage the cost of boots was reduced taking boots first strategies from a sure sign that you were bad to a viable strategy strong laners also got pushed out dominating the early game became effectively irrelevant as killing giant money bag heroes in the midgame would slingshot the trailing team into the lead the worst casualty has been the versatility of the game metas change and stuff goes in and out of favor that fine and fair but certain aspects have become imperative to have a support with a hard save a hard carry that can fight in the early mid game bad laning heroes can just be sent mid while traditional skill mid heroes are just sent to the safelane when you take a big lead the plan is almost always just farm out the map until you can t possibly lose when taking the high ground as taking a risk will not just result in you losing a fight but most likely the lead the game that i grew up with that punishes the smallest mistakes is a distant memory and we are left with a mid game nice
counter strike has always been more than just a tactical shooter it s a decades long conversation between players and the maps they ve memorized frame by frame stepping into cs feels like coming home to a house that s been beautifully renovated the layout is exactly how you remember it but the sunlight hits the floorboards in a way you ve never seen before
a new coat of paint on a classic canvas
the transition to the source engine is nothing short of breathtaking maps like inferno and overpass have been reimagined with a vibrancy that makes the world feel alive the way the light bounces off the cobblestones or reflects in the water isn t just a technical achievement it s an atmospheric shift that makes every round feel like a cinematic event
the magic of volumetric smoke
the most nostalgic yet revolutionary change is undoubtedly the responsive smoke grenades watching a smoke bloom and then seeing a hole carved through it by a well placed he grenade or a spray of bullets adds a layer of physical reality we only dreamed of back in the or source days it turns the ninja defuse and the smoke push into a dynamic game of cat and mouse that feels fresh every single time
that familiar rhythm
despite the upgrades the soul of the game remains untouched that specific shot of adrenaline when you re the last one alive in a v clutch the rhythmic clink of a perfect headshot and the frantic communication with teammates it s all there
sub tick updates while the technical side is complex the goal is simple making sure your shots land exactly when you click
the buy menu the new loadout system and circular menu feel like a modern evolution of the classic shopping experience keeping you focused on the strategy rather than the ui
final thoughts
cs manages to capture the lightning in a bottle feeling that has kept the franchise alive for over years it honors the legacy of the thousands of hours we spent in dusty hallways while providing a high fidelity playground for the next generation of legends it is a love letter to the competitive spirit polished punishing and utterly addictive

i had heard about counter strike for years but only started playing it in october last year in just a few months i ve already sunk over hours into it and i have zero regrets counter strike is in my opinion the purest competitive fps experience in the gaming world there are no fancy hero abilities no ultimate skills no rock paper scissors character counters what you have is raw skill pure decision making and intense gun play in those heart pounding clutch situations where the entire match is on the line my confidence doesn t come from some overpowered ability or hero advantage it comes from the countless hours i ve spent practicing my aim sharpening my game sense and learning perfect positioning every clutch win that seemed impossible every entry frag that opens up the site for the team it all feels incredibly rewarding every single second of every round gets my heart racing the tension is unmatched the satisfaction of outplaying the enemy through pure mechanics and smart plays is something no other shooter has ever given me counter strike has brought me countless moments of joy adrenaline and unforgettable memories with friends this game isn t just a hobby for me anymore i will keep loving counter strike for the rest of my life

once a great game now unplayable the matchmaking experience is easily one of the worst aspects games often feel wildly unbalanced with players of vastly different skill levels thrown into the same lobby it s not uncommon to see one team completely stomp the other with no real chance of a competitive match this ruins the core appeal of counter strike which has always been about tight skill based competition queue times don t justify the poor quality either you wait just as long only to end up in a match that feels decided before it even begins then there s the anti cheat system which frankly feels ineffective cheating has become far too noticeable especially in higher ranks and premier mode whether it s blatant wallhacks or more subtle aim assistance the lack of consistent enforcement makes it hard to take the competitive scene seriously when players feel like matches are being decided by cheaters rather than skill it completely kills motivation to play the premier points system only adds to the frustration the way points are gained or lost seems inconsistent and poorly explained you can perform well individually top frag and still lose a significant number of points just because your team lost overall counter strike currently struggles where it matters most fair competition between broken matchmaking weak anti cheat and a confusing ranking system it s hard to enjoy what should be a highly competitive and skill driven game

counter strike by valve is a modern update to one of the most iconic fps games ever made it keeps the classic tactical gameplay that fans love while introducing new features and improved graphics the best part of the game is its gameplay shooting feels accurate and every match requires skill teamwork and good strategy the new source engine makes the game look better with improved lighting and updated maps that still feel familiar however the game is not perfect many players feel that it launched with missing content compared to the previous version there are also bugs and performance issues that can affect the experience some changes have also been controversial especially among long time players the latest update brought new changes to gameplay including adjustments to weapons and mechanics one of the biggest changes is how reloading works making it more realistic but also frustrating for some players while the update adds more strategy not everyone likes these changes overall counter strike is still a strong competitive game with solid gameplay but it needs more improvements and better updates to satisfy all players rating

its csgo
counter strike review a beautiful upgrade held back by a familiar foe when valve announced the transition from cs go to counter strike the expectations were monumental cs go defined competitive shooters for a decade and stepping into the source era was a necessary evolution after spending countless hours in the new ecosystem it is clear that cs is fundamentally a fantastic game but it carries over some deeply frustrating legacy issues visuals and performance the source advantage the most immediate and striking change in cs is the visual overhaul the source engine breathes new life into the franchise pushing the frames with a ryzen and an rx xt the game looks absolutely gorgeous while maintaining the high refresh rates essential for competitive play the lighting overhauls on classic maps like inferno and overpass are stunning water physics reflections and material textures have all seen massive upgrades the biggest tactical shift comes from the new volumetric smokes they interact with the environment naturally expanding to fill spaces and reacting to gunfire and he grenades this single mechanic has completely refreshed site executions and defense strategies adding a dynamic layer to a game we ve known for years gameplay mechanics and the economy at its core the gunplay feels as satisfying and punishing as ever the spray patterns the crisp sound of a one tap and the intense pacing remain unmatched valve s introduction of the sub tick server architecture was intended to make movement and shooting feel perfectly synchronized while it had a rocky start it has steadily improved making engagements feel responsive and sharp the skin ecosystem a massive pillar of the counter strike experience also transitioned flawlessly for those of us deeply invested in the market whether it trading building personal collections or running a dedicated skin store seeing the inventories updated with the new lighting engine is a huge plus the skins simply pop more now preserving the vibrant economy that surrounds the game the elephant in the room the cheating epidemic despite all the mechanical and visual praises i can sing about cs there is a glaring issue that actively ruins the experience cheaters while the game itself is beautifully crafted the matchmaking experience particularly in premier mode is currently in a dismal state valve s anti cheat system vac live simply does not feel adequate hitting higher elo brackets currently feels like a coin toss on whether you will face a legitimate team or someone blatantly tracking through walls and aimbotting it is incredibly demoralizing to invest time into mastering the game mechanics only to lose points to software until valve implements a more intrusive or simply more effective anti cheat solution the competitive integrity of cs will remain severely compromised the verdict counter strike is without a doubt a great game it successfully modernizes a legendary formula without losing its soul the graphics are sharp the updated mechanics are deeply engaging and the foundation is solid however a competitive shooter is only as good as its competitive integrity pros stunning visual upgrades and lighting via the source engine game changing volumetric smoke mechanics the core gunplay remains the best in the fps genre skins and the economy look better than ever cons an overwhelming and unacceptable number of cheaters in matchmaking sub tick system still feels slightly inconsistent at times compared to native tick final score would be a if the cheating issue was resolved

cs is a brilliant game if you re into competition and long term progression at its core it s one of the most rewarding competitive shooters out there every match feels like it matters and improving actually comes down to your own skill aim positioning game sense when you win it feels earned when you lose you know exactly what you could ve done better what also keeps me coming back is the inventory system building up your inventory over time adds another layer to the experience whether it s unlocking skins trading or just slowly putting together a loadout you like it gives you something to work toward outside of just ranking up it s a nice balance between competitive focus and personal progression the gameplay itself is tight and consistent which is exactly what you want from a game like this it s easy to get into but very hard to master and that s what makes it so addictive a top tier competitive game and one that s just as satisfying outside the matches if you enjoy building up your inventory

factorio is a great game because it perfectly balances creativity problem solving and progression from the moment you start placing your first drills and conveyor belts you re pulled into a loop of designing optimizing and expanding your factory every small improvement whether it s reorganizing your smelting lines or automating a new component feels rewarding with hours already invested you ve likely experienced how the game constantly gives you just enough complexity to stay engaging without feeling overwhelming another reason factorio stands out is its depth and scalability what starts as a simple setup quickly evolves into a massive interconnected system where efficiency becomes an art form you can approach challenges in multiple ways whether you prefer neat organized layouts or sprawling chaotic megabases the game respects your playstyle while still pushing you to think critically about logistics resource management and long term planning that sense of growth from manual crafting to full automation is incredibly satisfying finally factorio s atmosphere and tension keep it exciting the constant threat of enemy attacks adds urgency to your expansion forcing you to balance defense with production at the same time the steady hum of machines and the visual flow of resources create a strangely relaxing rhythm it s a game that can be both intense and meditative often at the same time the factory never sleeps neither do the bugs

title you don t play factorio you exist across it
factorio starts as a simple factory builder but it doesn t stay that way for long
at first you operate in a microworld you place belts machines inserters you are directly involved in every action every piece matters and every decision is local
but as the factory grows something changes
you stop interacting with individual elements and start managing systems production lines train networks logistics chains everything becomes part of a larger structure you are no longer inside the factory in a traditional sense
you exist across it
in a strange way the game puts you into a kind of superposition you are present everywhere at once not physically but through design you are simultaneously dealing with iron shortages optimizing throughput expanding power and reworking logistics often across multiple locations or even planets
you are not the one doing the work anymore the system is
your role shifts from execution to orchestration
what makes this work is how transparent and fair the game is every problem has a clear cause every inefficiency can be traced there is no randomness hiding mistakes and no artificial delays masking bad design the feedback is immediate and honest
this creates a continuous loop of problem solution optimization new problem that is deeply engaging
and difficult to step away from
factorio has no natural stopping point you don t quit because you re finished you quit because you decide to stop one small fix turns into a complete redesign before you realize how much time has passed
i have spent thousands of hours in this game and the only real downside is this it is incredibly easy to lose yourself in it
in short if you enjoy systems efficiency and thinking at scale this is one of the best games ever made
just be aware once you stop being in the factory and start existing across it it s very hard to go back
friendly tip you will always need more green circuits
pure flow state beware time dilation
inifinite replayability superb impelmentation

in the grand scheme of things factorio is a giant puzzle game every challenge in the game can be solved by just connecting two buildings in the correct way with infinite space and resources at your hand and even zero time pressure if you play in peaceful mode once that done you might need to add more buildings so things can progress a little faster rinse and repeat eventually you ll find yourself in the middle of a sprawling factory it does not need to look clean or be perfectly balanced in order to be working in fact truly organically grown factories containing a lot of belt spaghetti even add to the puzzle element and consequently to the fun you can always clean up later or just move a bit to the left and just build a second factory
yes you can spend a lot of time rebuilding optimizing programming your own machinery through circuitry or add pressure by cranking up the enemies to play it as a brutal tower defense but all of that is optional once you got the hang of the base game there a huge amount of complete overhaul and quality of life mods to mold the game into a shape that more fitting to your playstyle the official space age dlc is basically just one of them so don t worry about that or it pricetag for now

i was initially skeptical of factorio because the vibe is kind of grim and before you learn the mechanics it can feel grindy however fundamentally this game is a masterclass in game design it reveals layer after layer of complexity as you re ready for it fractally expanding until the point that you ve built things you couldn t have conceived of now i m predisposed to love factorio since i love building things and thinking about systems factorio is basically systems thinking the game you re presented with an initial very simple system and you work through how to build and run it over and over you discover new problems and new tools for overcoming problems by the time you fully understand a problem and it starts to become uninteresting the game gives you a way to automate it away this is all true of the base game but if you enjoy that then i encourage you to come back after some time away and dig in to the space age expansion i was skeptical how much more they could add but it deftly adds a ton of new stuff in a way that stays interesting if you enjoy building and systems and iterating on stuff then factorio is a game for you my rated time of hours is certainly an over measurement from having left the game paused in the background overnight a number of times but it certainly one of my most played games of all time and i still love it i still haven t finished space age but am at a happy resting point and one day look forward to coming back and going further oh and don t sleep on the co op mode building things with other people is fun

this game is fantastic i wasn t really expecting much out of this game even after the positive things i ve heard about it but it so rare to see a game that while not being completely original excels at so much at what it tries to do
when i first played this game i felt that it was a cookie clicker meets tower defense game so i was already hooked what i didn t expect was an almost puzzle game like core gameplay loop introduced into the mix basically you play as an engineer who crash lands on a planet and has to build a rocket to escape you re given access to very little materials and even less knowledge you re also being attacked by the enemies in the game called biters and spitters the tower defense part you use a bunch of automation machines and setups in order to increase the speed productivity and efficiency to reach your goal of launching the rocket the cookie clicker part this core gameplay loop is actually deeper than that as it can be as simple as putting whatever device wherever it needed for the time being but being optimal is the name of the game so it better to find faster ways of placing machines in your base s without solely relying on the number of buildings or speed of individual buildings it an interesting setup since on modification to your base can have knock on effects in ways you may not be prepared for that where the puzzle part of it comes into play the core loop is deceptively simple but you can beat this game if you have enough patience and i find that inspiring
what i really appreciate about this games is that you re not going to get it right on the first try however that not expected of you and you get to progress at your own pace it makes future runs equally as enjoyable as your first run because of this the game teaches you to be patient with yourself if you re willing to learn and give you many tools to make it easier in a way that doesn t feel patronizing after all in this game just because someone gives you a setup that doesn t mean you re not responsible for making work nor does it mean it ll work well with everything else it also amazing how this game makes you feel so smart for making a single step if you get stuck and pause because you re confused or need to try to understand how something works better you re still making progress since you either have machines running in the background still producing stuff or the situation isn t dire enough to worry you
there very little negative i can say about this game most of the issues that i have with it is the fact that some upgrades are completely useless and some items are completely outclassed by others in a way that doesn t entirely work for me i ll spare the details since these are nitpicks for an otherwise amazing product
overall this game is fun and inspring a rare gem that you don t see too often definitely give it a shot

adjusts this goal by adding planets to the mix to reach this goal you have to build a factory what this means is not for the faint of heart if you value your life you basically have to progressively produce more enhanced materials as you research more and more complex technologies while also draining the planet of its resources to do this you start small building drills that require fuel and then refineries that refine the raw product into something else such as iron ore to steel plates that refined product is then turned into another product in a producer and so on it then only gets more complicated from there your goal throughout is to automate this entire process making things easier for you so you can focus on the other issue the bugs your factory produces pollution the inhabitants of the planet don t like the smell even though they choose to build their nests in the pollution and will attack your base if the pollution reaches them you can clear them out but as the game progresses they will get stronger and stronger and spread out more and more so if you take too long you may find yourself outgunned by the bugs very unlikely on unadjusted difficulty you may be a bit frustrated in the beginning trying to figure out how to fend of the insects while also keeping a solid flow within your factory most resource are transported on belts until you unlock the robot logistics system it a decent challenge which may cause you to consider going on the attack combat is simple enough basically just stock up on ammo and hold space to shoot while avoiding homing acid i know it tracks you i know it does don t tell me it doesn t but back to the main draw you will certainly be engrossed with growing your factory eventually you ll expand to getting oil then uranium building automated rail lines etc you might even decide you need a second base for more iron copper before you know it hours have passed h pros h list yeah i mean you don t need me to glaze this game engaging game for those interested in flow production automation i really like the variety in the resources that you can produce like it not just one thing that leads to another rather multiple things can eventually lead to or be produced from a resource i rarely found myself waiting around for research to finish there was always something to do whether it be killing insects or just expanding the factory soundtrack is haunting yet relaxing interrupted by your factory that is steadily polluting the environment i m bad at optimizing things but the game doesn t really punish you for it so long that it works i think it just takes longer list h cons h list now onto the biggest con i strongly believe that the game addiction factor is a detriment to its enjoyment before you laugh at me many of this review concerns the core factorio game and loop and not the space age dlc i feel that dlc deserves its own review which doesn t concern the core game hr hr factorio is the most well rounded game game i could have ever hoped for all without being overwhelming it features a very simple core loop extract resource create something from that resource use what you created to extract resources more efficiently that the whole loop similar to most survival crafting games inspired by minecraft this is all with the initial end goal of launching a rocket to space where it differs is how you apply resources and develop your game amongst the things you can make are machines that can automate the crafting process that means through a few simple steps you go from hand extracting and crafting resources to creating automated extraction and crafting tools to do all the work for you where games like minecraft ask you to stay in the initial loop of digging resources yourself for the entirety of the game factorio tells you to view everything around you as an automation problem to be solved and that is fun as hell if you enjoy problem solving as a game all of my play time in this game has been in two save files hours in the core factorio game hours of which i m not close to done yet in a space age save and i have to work hard to not fall into playing this game obsessively becuase it really is that much fun of a time sink i can easily avoid all my responsibilities in a day because i decided i needed to fix an item flow somewhere in my base because i now know better ways to do it or i might envision a train cargo system that automatically assigns trains to resource depots and i ve now spent hours straight doing exactly that by accident this is an incredible game and dangerously fun this barely mentions the fantastic art design brilliant music and sound effects research trees unique weapons and items you can create the constant sense of progression from the natural flow of the game and the endless ways to approach every problem it is a sandbox game with unique constraints that makes it endlessly more enjoyable in its own ways i always recommend to try the demo first to see if it for you and to introduce the core mechanics if you like it get the game itself it never on sale always and always will be at least at time of writing if you finish the core game launch a rocket and want a further nuanced goal with more challenging ways to play the game i suggest getting the space age dlc too but again only after you ve finished the core game once this is my favourite game ever made and it feels like it was personally devised for my specific niche i highly recommend it to anyone interested and caution you in the time you re about to spend best of luck that you need to refuel by hand as they slowly deliver you basic resources but before you know it you ve got a massive factory capable of automatically creating any material you could ever need spanning all across the map with train networks and automated defenses keeping your precious factory safe from the dangerous enemies i think the most genius part of this game is how the technologies all build on each other and how the core gameplay loop encourages you to keep trying to optimize and improve your factory this means that you always have many things you can do to improve how much your factory produces or how efficient it is you can always expand your science pack production to research things faster find a new ore patch or oil field to expand to improve your factory defenses or upgrade your furnace array if you re not careful it easy to get caught in a loop of saying oh i ll just do this one more thing for hours on end until you look at the clock and realize you ve been playing without interruption for the last hours but when you get to take a step back and just watch your factory work it so incredibly satisfying you can see a huge complicated network of transport belts mining drills pipes and assembling machines and know that you built everything yourself you know exactly how all the separate elements come together to create so many unique things and you still feel like you ve only breached the surface of the incredible depths this game has to offer all this and the dlc triples or quadruples the base game content and length if you like games that require factorio is a game about gathering resources crafting items and then ultimately automating crafting items there is a minor focus on combat this simply a mechanic to break up the monotony of crafting and providing a consequence to over expanding in the end once you have mastered the combat it can easily be disabled as it is more of a nuisance mind you the combat is not bad but its not very challenging on its own this is merely any obstacle to manage with your factory the main point of the base game is to automate the crafting of items you will start by crafting out base materials the gradually upgrade to more complex items to craft science items will need to be crafted to unlock new recipes with the ultimate goal of unlocking the recipe for crafting a rocket to send to space this is the ultimate goal of the base game now with all of this said i am at hrs of game play and i just now have starting using the most advanced items i was previously achievement hunting granted i have beaten the game much before now with much less than optimal play the truest goal of the game for most players is optimizing your factory for anyone interested in this game i highly recommend playing the demo this will give you access to the tutorial which took me about hours to complete this itself is almost a full game for free as far as how many hours you will get out of it if you love the game afterwards i would recommend you buy the game at full price as there are many many more hours of entertainment in the full game also the developers have previously mentioned the game will never be on sale as a side note i do not own the dlc and i have not played any mods there are many more hours of content to enjoy as the modding community is very strong

recommended playtime hours i m starting yet another new factorio playthrough and at this point i ve completely lost track of how many factories i ve built torn down rebuilt optimized and then rebuilt again because i realized i could squeeze out more efficiency with over hours played i can confidently say this is one of the best designed games i ve ever touched factorio is deceptively simple at the start mine resources automate production research technology but it very quickly turns into a deep endlessly complex logistics puzzle where every solution creates two new problems you want to solve there s always a bottleneck somewhere always a layout that could be cleaner always a system that technically works but offends you on a spiritual level because you know it could be better what really sets factorio apart is how rewarding it feels to learn the game doesn t hold your hand but it gives you all the tools you need to succeed when you finally understand ratios trains circuit logic or oil processing it feels earned mistakes aren t just allowed they re part of the process every messy early factory becomes the blueprint for a cleaner smarter one later the sense of progression is excellent you start hand feeding machines and end up orchestrating massive self sustaining production lines that span the map watching your factory grow from chaos into something relatively elegant is incredibly satisfying and if you enjoy optimization planning and problem solving this game will absolutely consume your free time without you realizing it even after hundreds of hours factorio never really runs out of things to do different map settings self imposed challenges megabases speedruns or just trying a this time i ll do it right run keep it fresh and that s before even touching mods which add an absurd amount of replayability on their own factorio isn t flashy it doesn t rely on cutscenes or story beats what it does have is near perfect mechanics rock solid performance and an incredibly addictive gameplay loop if you enjoy games that respect your intelligence and reward patience and planning this is an easy recommendation the factory must grow and it always will

b factorio b is hailed as one of the original automation games the epitome of automation big brain thinking big factory layouts and consuming massive quantities it is difficult to think small when thinking inside or about factorio this game is also one of the few where the developers have a hard stance on b never participating in a sale of any kind b after four years of early access five years on market and one massive expansive dlc later where does the game stand today b u the good u b list the artwork in this game is fantastic and holds up at multiple zoom levels which is technically impressive for the game engine itself this feature is also vital for quickly glancing at the factory and sussing out what comes next the artwork is also very unique and there is nothing else on the market quite like it this lends a lot to the character of the game as looking at the factory in motion is primarily what most players end up doing at one point or another the game engine runs fairly well despite the eventual immense scale of most factories blueprinting layouts can easily be handled in a sandbox environment then imported into current saves this not only saves time but can help facilitate better understanding of layouts and play the community can also share blueprints for easier new player approaches logistical challenges are present and require forethought to some degree automation through trains and rail networks is handled well and can be a lot of fun trains can also become unplanned defensive mechanisms or errant player deaths list b u the mediocre u b list the soundtrack is unobtrusive but unmemorable factorio can lend itself well to being something to do while listening to an audio book or lengthy video biters the antagonist aliens in the main game are intelligent and require thought to deal with however they cannot be sent through a maze like a tower defense options to deal with them are minimal at best and unexciting at worst combat can be too fast at times leading to the player dying as the biters out damage player repair kits or player damage output while logistical challenges are present they are simply fixed by adding b more things b until problems are solved fun is relative either the biters are the entertainment or throwing oneself against the myriad of design and layout issues is the entertainment if neither of these things are entertaining i nothing is entertaining i list b u the bad u b list the game scales poorly when starting out the first challenge is to get automation up and running as that is the soul of the game this is handled by pouring resources into creating science packs and unlocking technology this is the core game loop for progression however after completing red and green science pseudo tutorial to science and research the next steps become horrendously expensive want red and green science pack factories using a factorio calculator this gives a minimum of stone furnaces electric mining drills and assemblers to produce red science and green science per minute now for the equivalent blue science packs per minute the next automation tier an additional stone furnaces electric mining drills new oil processing and assemblers are needed b i and most likely new resource patches trains and assembling train tracks i b this is using just tier automation machines however tier machines shrink the footprint steel furnaces and tier assemblers the drills are already tier none of this addresses throughput and the limitations of the conveyor belts the above means factory layouts become massive quickly this would not be such an issue if factorio had this information displayed in some means the player can figure out however it does not often times players utilize outside of game tools and utilities to math out what the factory needs and how to meet the minimum requirements a simple in game calculator mod disables achievements if those are important to you this seems like something the developers could have addressed in ten years but still choose not to for some reason while trying to figure out massive factory layout requirements biters are an ever present threat playing on default settings these little annoyances quickly grow into powerful distractions threatening to end the game they expand frequently and can grow in strength rapidly dealing with them directly only amplifies their strength growth requiring the player to constantly keep ahead in defensive research and funnel an ever increasing amount of resources to keep them at bay the massive layout requirements demand the player eventually push them back and deal with them which in turn only amplifies their danger this is a death spiral for newer players if a player stays ahead of biter issues they become a mere nuisance rather than an engaging element of the game this begs the question as to why they exist in the first place other than to serve as punishment for new players and an uninteresting engagement for seasoned veterans b i i have read several threads in which veterans usually shut biters off eventually due to performance issues in the late game as well i b there are additional issues with automation for balancing resources on belts to handle throughput problems and the insertion tools that put things into the many buildings often fail to have the reach necessary to grab the items with h would you recommend this game to other players well h that what steam asks me when i post a review and for factorio as much as it goes against the grain i m going to have to say no unfortunately h but what about the positives it can t be all bad h that is definitely true some standouts the amount of qol features present is something other games in the genre should strive for the optimization and developer transparency is second to none in the industry and should be displayed as an example of how you develop software and keep your community informed it runs flawlessly under linux without the need for proton compatibility layers thanks to having a native linux build h but we re not here to review software design practices h unfortunately the game is marred by some questionable pricing and design choices the elephant in the room first the pricing i bought this game back when it was much cheaper sometime back in and i d argue that a great price for this game given the content on display about hours for a playthrough if you take your time but looking at it now with its current price tag i cannot recommend it while yes i may seem a tad hypocritical with my hours in this game aside from a bit of mucking around in multiplayer most of those hours consisted of a much more clueless version of me bouncing off this game repeatedly over the years before finally sitting down and the game seriously only to be beat the base game underwhelmed and go wait that it and what in the base game for a game that advertises itself as a logistics sim there little in the way of complex logistics required to actually beat the game look at a diagram of a printed circuit board and you ve already solved the game biggest logistical challenge massing resources and splitting them off where they need to go i had hoped that maybe the mathematical side of the game could change things but no it all stuff you could solve in minutes with algebra you d learn in secondary school there an entire digital logic system you can play around with but aside from one optional case which i found quite fun granted it has next to no practical use when it comes to your main goal of launching a rocket so how do we make an easy game harder h solution grab a hammer h every hour or every half hour if you re unlucky the fine residents of the planet will decide to waltz up to your buildings with an assortment of instruments of deconstruction and subject you to forced rapid disassembly of course jests aside the biters feel like an impedance and an afterthought to pad out a simple game with more uninteresting busywork clear their nests with a shallow combat system whose automation comes too late mindlessly build defences by clicking and dragging straight lines of belts full of items whose recipes are so simple you can just mindlessly plop down factories making them without second thought or just turn them off and live a happier life without their constant tantrums h is what i would say if h the game weren t designed around them existing there exists an entire research tree dedicated to killing them better and there an entire crafting tab dedicated to making the gear that kills them faster h but what about mods h admittedly i didn t touch mods and truthfully they shouldn t be taken into consideration when reviewing a standalone game such as this this game is not advertised as a modding platform and thus it should be judged for what it provides mods may eclipse the quality of the base game yes but they don t render any verdict on the base game quality moot h verdict h it a great piece of software but as a game it stands marred with game design choices that are either frustratingly simple or frustratingly inconvenient spend your money elsewhere

a prime example of gaming done right at first glance it seems simple a factory building game where you are attempting to automate production of materials which you will use to produce further items or conduct research but the genius behind the implementation is just how many ways you can perform that task excellent player expression you are given a blank slate to do with as you please a single prompt to start the game you are here on an unknown planet you play build and explore the whole time you feel like you are discovering something new and interesting the base game of just building a rocket is already a great taste of what the game has to offer but then space age my goodness it takes it up to you are not just building a rocket anymore you are traveling the stars settling strange new planets and learning unique and challenging new puzzles on each one
then you realize the game has an amazing mod framework with well documented api if space age takes the base game to mods takes it to i have never seen a game which supports its modding community like this easily install update and manage your mods from inside the game easily swap between mod sets for different save files with convenient buttons for syncing which mods are enabled as well as their options to reflect the settings for that save then outside the game they have an entire database documenting everything related to the mod framework and its prototypes if you want to modify something its as easy as looking it up and doing it not to mention the developer keybindings you can use in game as well
